add_namespace = election

country_event = {
	id = election.2
	title = election.2.t
	desc = election.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_airplane_factory

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			OR = {
				has_war = yes
				any_neighbor_country = {
					has_war = yes
				}
				any_allied_country = {
					has_war = yes
				}
			}
		}
		has_idea = partial_economic_mobilisation
	}

	option = {
		name = election.2.a
		ai_chance = { 
			base = 1
		}
		add_ideas = low_economic_mobilisation

	}

	option = {
		name = election.2.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				can_lose_unity = yes
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05

		add_war_support = -0.05

	}
}

country_event = {
	id = election.3
	title = election.3.t
	desc = election.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_tank_factory

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_government = democratic
		has_war = no
		OR = {
			any_neighbor_country = {
				has_war = yes
			}
			any_allied_country = {
				has_war = yes
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_idea = low_economic_mobilisation
			has_idea = civilian_economy
			has_idea = isolation
			has_idea = undisturbed_isolation
			has_idea = volunteer_only
			has_idea = disarmed_nation
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = election.3.a
		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = low_economic_mobilisation }
			add_ideas = partial_economic_mobilisation
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = civilian_economy }
			add_ideas = low_economic_mobilisation
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = isolation }
			add_ideas = civilian_economy
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = undisturbed_isolation }
			add_ideas = isolation
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = volunteer_only }
			add_ideas = limited_conscription
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_idea = disarmed_nation }
			add_ideas = volunteer_only
		}

		add_war_support = 0.05

	}

	option = {
		name = election.3.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		add_stability = -0.05

	}
}

country_event = {
	id = election.4
	title = election.4.t
	desc = election.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_usa_election_generic

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = AFG
		OR = {
			democratic > 0.5
			neutrality > 0.5
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = election.4a
		set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = AFG_conservative_party name = AFG_conservative_party }
		retire_country_leader = yes
		set_country_leader_ideology = conservatism
	}

	option = {
		name = election.4b
		set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = AFG_liberal_party name = AFG_liberal_party }
		retire_country_leader = yes
		set_country_leader_ideology = liberalism
	}

	option = {
		name = election.4c
		set_party_name = { ideology = democratic long_name = AFG_liberal_2_party name = AFG_liberal_2_party }
		retire_country_leader = yes
		set_country_leader_ideology = liberalism
	}
}
